<section id="content" style="width: 100%;">
					<div id="post-20934" class="post-20934 page type-page status-publish hentry">
			
			
			<div class="post-content">
				<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-1 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;--awb-flex-wrap:wrap;"><div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start fusion-flex-justify-content-center fusion-flex-content-wrap" style="max-width:1248px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );"><div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-0 fusion_builder_column_2_3 2_3 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:66.666666666667%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:2.88%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:0px;--awb-spacing-left-large:2.88%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;"><div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column"><div class="fusion-text fusion-text-1" style="--awb-content-alignment:justify;"><h2><strong>Our Little Giving Artists raised $12,000 for AWWA this year</strong></h2>
<p>The Skool4Kidz ‘Little Giving Artists’ community outreach fund-raising campaign is now into its third year. The amount will be donated to AWWA for the less fortunate children under its care.</p>
<p>‘Little Giving Artists’ is a fundraising initiative by Skool4Kidz Care Fund, the corporate social responsibility arm which promotes inclusiveness in the children’s early years learning. The exercise allows our children learn at a young age to be selfless and to show compassion to their less fortunate peers in the community.</p>
<p>It engaged children from our Art Enrichment Programme across Skool4Kidz Preschool’s Nursery to Kindergarten children in a creative exercise with the theme “Nature &amp; I”. Skool4Kidz worked with experienced art educators from Crestar Learning Centre to guide the children in painting nature-related images on sustainable bags using an acrylic medium.</p>
</div><div class="fusion-image-element " style="text-align:center;--awb-margin-bottom:20px;--awb-caption-title-font-family:var(--h2_typography-font-family);--awb-caption-title-font-weight:var(--h2_typography-font-weight);--awb-caption-title-font-style:var(--h2_typography-font-style);--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-1 hover-type-none"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" width="1200" height="748" title="LGA-2023-photo" src="https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1.jpg" data-orig-src="https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1.jpg" alt="" class="img-responsive wp-image-23616 lazyautosizes ls-is-cached lazyloaded" srcset="https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1-200x125.jpg 200w, https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1-400x249.jpg 400w, https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1-600x374.jpg 600w, https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1-800x499.jpg 800w, https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1.jpg 1200w" data-srcset="https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1-200x125.jpg 200w, https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1-400x249.jpg 400w, https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1-600x374.jpg 600w, https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1-800x499.jpg 800w, https://skool4kidz.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/LGA-2023-photo-1.jpg 1200w" data-sizes="auto" data-orig-sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" sizes="719px"></span></div><div class="fusion-text fusion-text-2"><p>A total of 182 bags were painted in the month-long exercise, which help to inculcate values of compassion and the spirit of giving in our children. Images of the bags will be featured in an art gallery at the bottom of this page.</p>
<p>Images of the bags are featured in an art gallery at the bottom of this page.</p>
<p>Members of the Skool4Kidz’ family, relatives and friends were invited to donate a minimum of $30 each time via <a href="https://www.giving.sg/campaigns/littlegivingartists2023" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Giving.sg</a> towards this cause.</p>
<p>The children raised a total of $12,000 for AWWA Kindle Garden Preschool, so that young learners with additional needs, hearing and visual impairment can enjoy quality early childhood education.</p>
</div><div class="fusion-image-element " style="text-align:center;--awb-margin-bottom:20px;--awb-caption-title-font-family:var(--h2_typography-font-family);--awb-caption-title-font-weight:var(--h2_typography-font-weight);--awb-caption-title-font-style:var(--h2_typography-font-style);--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span $(document).ready(function(){
    var url = new URL(window.location); // Construct URL object using current browser URL
    var params = url.searchParams; // Get query parameters object
    var S4Kcentre = params.get("S4Kcentre"); // Get value of S4Kcentre
    $("#S4Kcentre").val(S4Kcentre); // Set it as the dropdown value
    $("select").change(function(){
        $(this).find("option:selected").each(function(){
            var optionValue = $(this).attr("value");
            window.history.replaceState(null, null, "?S4Kcentre=" + optionValue);
            if(optionValue){
                $(".centre").not("." + optionValue).hide();
                $("." + optionValue).show();
            }
        });
    }).change();
});
